</header><div class="entry-content"><div class="tasty-pins-hidden-image-container" style="display:none;"><img alt="Mahi mahi cooking on a grill pan and in a platter of tacos for gluten-free fish taco night" class="tasty-pins-hidden-image" data-pin-description="AMAZING Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw! 30 min, 10 ingredients, served with Spicy Chipotle Aioli! #dinner #tacos #fish #glutenfree #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/MB-GrilledFishTacos-Pinterest-1.jpg" data-pin-title="Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw (30 Minutes!)" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/06/MB-GrilledFishTacos-Pinterest-1-200x200.jpg"/></div>

<p>Summer weather is upon us in our part of the world and that means one thing to us: Grilling season!</p>
<p>These grilled fish tacos are my take on the fish tacos we’ve enjoyed while traveling to beach towns where the fish is fresh, the tortillas tender, and the salsa light and flavorful. Plus, just <strong>10 customizable ingredients</strong> and <strong>30 minutes</strong> required! Let’s do this.</p>
<p><img alt="Assortment of ingredients for making Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw" class="aligncenter wp-image-43519 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw (30 Minutes!)" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe.jpg" data-pin-description="AMAZING Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw! 30 min, 10 ingredients, served with Spicy Chipotle Aioli! #dinner #tacos #fish #glutenfree #minimalistbaker #recipe" data-pin-title="Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw (30 Minutes!)" height="2098" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe-208x300.jpg 208w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe-768x1107.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe-711x1024.jpg 711w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe-600x865.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/05/AMAZING-Grilled-Fish-Tacos-with-Pineapple-Cabbage-Slaw-30-min-10-ing-served-with-Spicy-Chipotle-Aioli-dinner-tacos-fish-glutenfree-minimalistbaker-recipe-680x980.jpg 680w" width="1456"/><span id="more-43488"></span></p>
<h3>Best Fish for Fish Tacos?</h3>
<p>The best fish for fish tacos tends to be flaky, tender white fish, such as tilapia, snapper, grouper, cod, halibut, mahi-mahi, or black drum.</p>
<p>We ended up going with mahi-mahi, which is incredibly light and flaky. I also include some suggestions below for vegan alternatives.</p>
<p>For seasoning, I kept things super simple with a little oil, salt, and chili powder. I also tested a batch rolled in fine cornmeal, which added a delightful crunch! Certainly optional but a fun variation for more texture.</p>
<p>For those who don’t have a grill, you can just as easily cook inside using a <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/QvrzcgqsfgPwtbR44m2XLP4AAAFqmG9aaQEAAAFKAduS6BU/https://www.amazon.com/Lodge-Square-Ribbed-12-Inch-Handles/dp/B0001DJVGA/?creativeASIN=B0001DJVGA&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=IYA2nWmFC2dyIwymdlnxhw&amp;slotNum=2&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer" target="_blank">grill pan like this one</a> or just opt for a <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Quo_OZCIJypUU2UGKJ1cpt8AAAFqmO4IeAEAAAFKAVwnUq8/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00IWSQCI6/?creativeASIN=B00IWSQCI6&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=g9yVTLeNzowCGvRoCNkDPQ&amp;slotNum=25&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer" target="_blank">cast iron skillet</a>.</p>

<p><iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/orl4UUGcjp0" width="680"></iframe></p>
<h3>Best Slaw for Fish Tacos?</h3>
<p>For fish tacos that are seasoned with a little spice (such as chili powder), it’s nice to have a little acidity (such as lime) and sweetness (such as pineapple) to balance out the flavors. So we mixed up some <strong>chopped pineapple, onion, cilantro, cabbage, and lime juice</strong>.</p>
<p>You could easily sub mango for the pineapple, or throw in a jalapeño or serrano pepper for some more heat. Or, in a pinch, just whip up a simple <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/vegan-7-layer-mexican-dip/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">pico de gallo</a>.</p>

<p>We hope you LOVE these tacos! They’re:</p>
<p>Simple<br/>
Savory-sweet<br/>
Fresh<br/>
Customizable<br/>
Satisfying<br/>
&amp; Delicious</p>
<p>These tacos would make the perfect meal when you need something fresh and satisfying on the table fast. They’re ideal for summer and pair beautifully with <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/baked-plantain-chips-garlicky-guacamole/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Garlicky Guacamole and Plantain Chips</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/5-ingredient-ginger-beer-margaritas/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">5-Ingredient Ginger Beer Margaritas</a>, and <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/mexican-pinto-beans-scratch-1-pot/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">1-Pot Mexican Pinto Beans</a>.</p>
<p>Into tacos? Be sure to check out our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/panko-baked-avocado-tacos/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Crunchy Avocado Tacos</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/saucy-portobello-butternut-squash-tacos/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Smoky Portobello Butternut Squash Tacos</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/roasted-cauliflower-tacos-with-chipotle-romesco/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Roasted Cauliflower Tacos with Chipotle Romesco</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/spicy-plantain-black-bean-tacos/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Spicy Black Bean Plantain Tacos</a>, and <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/roasted-vegetable-tacos-chimichurri/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Roasted Vegetable Tacos with Chimichurri</a>!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Grilled Fish Tacos with Pineapple Cabbage Slaw</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
<p>Quick &amp; easy grilled fish tacos with pineapple-cabbage slaw and creamy chipotle aioli! Light flavors, perfect for grilling season and beyond! Just 10 ingredients and 30 minutes required.</p> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>

<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="43489" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> - <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="43489" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">FOR SERVING</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">batch</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/5-ingredient-chipotle-aioli/" target="_blank">Chipotle Aioli</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<strong><em>optional </em></strong>// see notes for a quicker, nut-free substitution)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">6</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">medium</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">corn tortillas </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(use grain-free tortillas as needed // or sub flour tortillas)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Lime wedges</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">FISH</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">lb</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">white fish filets* </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(such as tilapia, snapper, grouper, cod, halibut, mahi-mahi, or black drum)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">avocado oil </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or other neutral cooking oil // plus more for oiling grill or grill-pan)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sea salt</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chili powder</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4 </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">fine cornmeal</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<strong><em>optional </em></strong>// see notes for tips on achieving added crunch)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">PINEAPPLE SLAW</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">diced fresh pineapple </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(use fresh, or you could grill your pineapple with your fish for more flavor)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">thinly shredded red cabbage</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">finely diced red onion</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">finely chopped cilantro</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">lime juice</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">healthy pinch</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sea salt</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>If preparing optional chipotle aioli, do so at this time. Set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Slice fish into medium bite-size pieces or long strips (skin removed) and add to a plate. Drizzle with avocado oil and toss to coat. Then season both sides liberally with sea salt and chili powder and dust with cornmeal (optional for added crunch). You want the fish to be well seasoned, so don't hold back! Once seasoned, set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Prepare slaw by adding pineapple, cabbage, red onion, cilantro, lime, and sea salt to a medium mixing bowl and tossing to combine. Set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Heat a grill, or heat a <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/QiIS3MvnJa-Q2FCG0H46T_8AAAFqfzzHXAEAAAFKARLJQZQ/https://www.amazon.com/Lodge-Square-Ribbed-12-Inch-Handles/dp/B0001DJVGA/?creativeASIN=B0001DJVGA&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=bqAeQbnYaTS1mA.nHEtpOQ&amp;slotNum=9&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">grill pan</a> or <a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/Quo_OZCIJypUU2UGKJ1cpt8AAAFqmO4IeAEAAAFKAVwnUq8/https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00IWSQCI6/?creativeASIN=B00IWSQCI6&amp;linkCode=w61&amp;imprToken=g9yVTLeNzowCGvRoCNkDPQ&amp;slotNum=25&amp;tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">cast iron skillet</a> over medium-high heat. Brush the surface with a little oil to prevent sticking.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Once the grill or grill pan is hot, add the seasoned fish and let cook for 3-4 minutes (without moving), or until grill marks are visible and the underside appears cooked (check the underside gently to avoid tearing). Then gently flip using a spatula or tongs. Handle the fish carefully as white fish can be tender.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Cook for another 1-2 minutes, or until the middle appears cooked and the underside also has grill marks. Set aside and cover to keep warm until serving.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><b><i>Optional:</i></b> Warm tortillas by wrapping in a damp towel or paper towel and heating in the microwave for 30 seconds, or in a 400 degree F (204 C) oven for 5 minutes or until warm.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>To serve, divide fish between tortillas and top with slaw, fresh lime juice, and aioli (optional but recommended for bigger flavor!).</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Best when fresh. Slaw will keep in the refrigerator up to 3-4 days. Aioli will keep in the refrigerator for 1 week. Fish can be stored in the refrigerator up to 2-3 days. Reheat in the microwave or on the stovetop until hot. Not freezer friendly.</p></div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-video-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header"></h3>
<iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/orl4UUGcjp0" width="680"></iframe> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-notes-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Notes</h3>
<p>*If you don’t want to make aioli or are nut sensitive, you can sub 3/4 cup (173 g) sour cream (dairy-free as needed) + 1 chopped chipotle pepper in adobo sauce + 1-2 Tbsp (15-30 ml) lime juice and stir to combine.<br/>*As far as fish goes, do your best to <strong>source a high-quality, saltwater fish</strong> that’s not farmed. <br/>*<strong>To keep this recipe vegan</strong>, you can sub the fish for seasoned grilled <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/quick-easy-crispy-tofu/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">tofu</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/spicy-jackfruit-tacos-1-pot-meal/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">smoky jackfruit</a>, or <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-tempeh-burrito-bowls/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">tempeh</a>. <br/>*Nutrition information is a rough estimate calculated with mahi-mahi, the lesser amount of lime juice, and without optional ingredients. <br/>*Inspiration from the <a href="https://cooking.nytimes.com/recipes/1012445-fish-tacos?action=click&amp;module=Global%20Search%20Recipe%20Card&amp;pgType=search&amp;rank=1" rel="noopener" target="_blank">New York Times</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-nutrition-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Nutrition Per Serving (1 of 6 tacos) </h3><ul><li><strong>Calories:</strong> 157 <li><strong>Fat:</strong> 3.6g <li><strong>Saturated fat:</strong> 0.5g <li><strong>Sodium:</strong> 403mg <li><strong>Potassium:</strong> 447mg <li><strong>Carbohydrates:</strong> 14.8g <li><strong>Fiber:</strong> 2g <li><strong>Sugar:</strong> 2.8g <li><strong>Protein:</strong> 16.7g</li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></ul> </div>

<p>My husband claims he never liked fish until the is recipe! The first time we made it, we were in a rush and left off the slaw (what a mistake!), but the second time, we added it in and WOW. I second the other folks who said they felt like they were at a restaurant. It also kept wonderfully for lunch the next day!</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-832690">October 4, 2019 at 9:04 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I feel like I’m in a restaurant!! These are AMAZING! So flavorful, definitely include the Chipotle Aioli.  Usually when I make fish tacos I season the fish and leave it whole, because then you can break it up later and fish like cod will fall apart when you flip it anyway. This time I tried cutting the fish up first, but then ended up with mush in the pan. Doesn’t affect the flavor though! I think for a vegan option these would for sure be equally as good with the jackfruit option.</p>

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Nat" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/f43ef083d722b270bf41b5a10d3a2f36?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/f43ef083d722b270bf41b5a10d3a2f36?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Nat" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Nat</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-829632">September 21, 2019 at 7:00 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This vegan hate is crazy. Dana never marketed this blog as vegan and I (as a vegan) just feel lucky to have access to a plethora of amazing recipes that are FREE and so tasty (never had a bad one!). If you read the recipe Dana not only suggests vegan alternatives to the fish but also makes a note of sourcing the fish sustainably. What more could you want?! Vegans need to get off their high horses and realise that for some people (for example a large part of my family who are subsistence fisherman) eating meat is a non-negotiable part of life. Reducing consumption and making sure that it is sustainable as possible is important but these are two things that Dana does in this recipe and throughout her blog. You should be celebrating her work and efforts or at the very least not click on a recipe that’s clearly labeled ‘Fish Tacos’. </p>
<p>I’m really looking forward to trying these (maybe with jackfruit as I haven’t cooked with it much) and I’d just like to thank you Dana for being such an amazing cook and sharing your recipes freely.</p>
</div>

<p>Hi Riley, thanks for the feedback. We will still continue producing plenty of plant-based recipes alongside new recipes with eggs and meat. If you’d prefer to only see the vegan recipes, you can subscribe to our vegan-only recipe email list (modify your subscription at the bottom of any email we’ve sent you). Or visit our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/recipe-index" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">recipe page</a> and select “special diet” and “vegan” to display all vegan recipes.</p>

<p>I just wanted to shout out and say thank you for providing me with years and years of allergen-free and vegan and vegetarian friendly recipes. Your website has been my go-to as I’ve found out about allergies and eliminated various animal products from my diet. </p>
<p>Tacos are one of my favourite things and I can’t resist a good slaw, so I will definitely be using this recipe for my next taco night. I am especially grateful for suggestions on how to make this recipe vegan as I eliminated all animal products from my diet earlier this year.</p>
<p>Most of all, thank you for promoting healthy eating and not just veganism. A vegan lifestyle is not always accessible for all people, so I think it is great to provide people with recipes that offer alternatives and hopefully in the process they will discover some of your amazing plant-based recipes.</p>
<p>I have been for years and I will continue to tell any one who is willing to listen about your website.</p>
<p>Thanks again for helping me on my food journey!</p>
</div>

<p>I am so happy to see healthy and interesting recipes including fish:)<br/>
Really looking forward to try this dish and I would like to wish you good luck! </p>
<p>To all these rude vegans:<br/>
Recently I started incorporating fish in my meals too, because I can’t fight this b12 deficiency battle anymore and must admit – I have always had a craving for fish and seafood. Not that I feel much better now, but my skin got clearer and even got skinnier. Everyone’s body is different and to be healthy is my priority! You don’t have to consume meat daily or even weekly, because we do in fact consume meat way too much (not to mention how much it affects the environment), but I’d rather include fish in my meals than buy vegan alternatives that are not healthy at all.<br/>
Much love to you all ;)</p>

Amy</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Denise" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/5ffedc8cd79c17d2633228ff58c39b4a?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/5ffedc8cd79c17d2633228ff58c39b4a?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Denise" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Denise</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-811750">July 3, 2019 at 1:51 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I must say that this blog is one of the most beautiful and truly resourceful site I have EVER used. Her recipes are not only accurate. But really helped me when I was diagnosed with my long list of food allergies which include eggs, bananas, pecans, peaches, gluten and most diary.  Anyone who has a gluten intolerance or food allergies also use this site for ideas and a way to be able to enjoy the meals we miss once living with these food intolerances.  I personally as well am a flexible eater but my body is happier eating a plant based diet. But I must admit that I once was a Ugly Teen Vegan who was rude, judgmental, and just plain mean when it came to expressing my veganism and why it was right. I personally feel so happy that I follow a blog as amazing as this, because it follows what I believe in and try to implement in my life, which is put your body and health first. I began listening to my body and now I eat a nice balance of plant based meals and occasionally some fish or local animal protein . I am definitely am not blinded to all the horribleness that is happening in our world in the food industry. But if we can all focus on remembering that everyones body is different and needs different things then we can all live and bring a little more happiness, positivity, and peace to this small world.</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-810807">
<article id="article-comment-810807">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Dominique Hellmich" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/0641255483923e6c2b94a2376ed4eb70?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/0641255483923e6c2b94a2376ed4eb70?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Dominique Hellmich" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Dominique Hellmich</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-810807">June 27, 2019 at 10:30 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Dana, </p>
<p>First I wanna say DANG! these tacos were on point! My boyfriend does not like fish so I usually only get to eat fish tacos at restaurants. However, this year I’ve been trying to shift the meat-component of my flexitarian diet to sustainable seafood, so I’ve been looking for ways to train his palate to be more accepting of ocean critters. He is Mexican so there is always a special place in his heart for tacos. He wouldn’t mind if we ate them 5x a week! I LOVE the combo of pineapple + chipotle so when I saw this recipe I needed to give it a shot. We made it with cod on the electric grill and it turned out great! The fish-hating BF ate it with lots of extra aioli, but got second helpings in the end. :) </p>
<p>Second, THANK YOU for years of quality, delicious, and plant-based content. I stumbled upon your site years ago when a google search turned up your 5 ingredient granola bars (still a staple in our house). This was back in my college days when I was just starting to take the first steps from serious carnivore, to a more plant-based diet. I grew up in a family that cooked meat for dinner every night, made bacon for breakfast in the morning, and sent us off to school with turkey sandwiches for lunch. I didn’t know there could be a world of cooking outside of meat, eggs, and dairy. Being a dirt-poor college student demanded change, but for this naive cook “going vegetarian” meant many nights of pasta with jarred marinara sauce. Then I moved into a house with a variety of vegetarian, flexitarian, and vegan friends. We cooked communal dinners so when it was my turn at the chopping block I needed recipe inspiration FAST. Your website was one of the invaluable few that taught me just how easy and delicious plant-based recipes can be. </p>
<p>It’s frustrating to see people being so angry and close-minded about you adding a few meat recipes to your site, when the reality is you don’t owe anything to ANYONE. You’ve created so much amazing content that you could have sequestered away from the world. Instead you decided to share it and help people like me learn that there are better (more health and environmentally conscious) ways to live and eat! I’m sure I’m not the only person whose relationship with food you’ve help change for the better. So thank you for everything so far, and keep on rockin’ girl!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Very tasty tacos. I used thawed frozen cod fillets and fried in a cast iron pan. They stuck a bit but that didn’t affect the flavour. I followed the recipe except I omitted the red onion (hubby doesn’t care for it). The aioli was good and spicy. Loved it. I added too much salt to my slaw but that was my fault. I was hoping for a little leftover for a snack for the next day, but we polished it up just the 2 of us.  Thanks for the recipe. A keeper.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Dom,<br/>
To answer your question about my exposure to other countries… I hold citizenship in two countries, lived in several countries, an avid traveler plus I’m a published travel author.<br/>
Vegan/vegetarianism is the fastest growing segment of the food industry. Had you invested in some of the market’s biggest faux meat produces in the past year you would of seen a return in excess of 250%. So yes, non meat diets are the future and growing, minimalist baker is taking a step into the archaic past by abandoning this reality. I’m assuming this is being done purely for financial reasons.</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Francesca" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/ec3fe78f8514fb9f9616f2b8962467f3?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/ec3fe78f8514fb9f9616f2b8962467f3?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Francesca" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Francesca</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-812055">July 5, 2019 at 8:50 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>It’s because, unfortunately, vegan diets do not provide what is needed for optimal health for most people.  There are so many nutrients which, in their plant forms, are slowly being found to be insufficient.  This is why so many vegans either cheat on their diets or revert back to eating some animal products after developing health issues over several years.  If you are eating dairy and eggs as a vegetarian, you have a better chance of success but only if these are high quality (pastured) products.</p>
</div>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>These sound absolutely scrumptious, especially after a warm summer day when you want something refreshing but quick. I will definitely be making these!</p>
<p>I strongly advise against tilapia, though.  It’s farmed, and not under very sanitary conditions. The fish are raised in over-populated and over-polluted tanks.</p>
<p>But back to the tacos:  I can’t wait to try these, and the coleslaw, also!  Thanks!</p>

<img alt="Avatar for T" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/cc3c9749f364612b7b02bebf39fae9f8?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/cc3c9749f364612b7b02bebf39fae9f8?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for T" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">T</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-809034">June 17, 2019 at 2:21 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I appreciate all you do, and as a vegan I don’t feel unwelcome that you include non-vegan recipes.   I can ignore them, just like I ignore the animal recipes in other cookbooks and on other sites.   And I do appreciate how far you go to make great vegan recipes available, and appreciate your accommodating us in your email list and in your recipe index.</p>
<p>I do find it easier to understand the inclusion of the occasional egg or some cheese than to actually include flesh.   But again, it is your blog to post what you wish, and I enormously appreciate all the fantastic vegan recipes you post.</p>
<p>But still, while I don’t have any right to complain, I do feel a certain sadness in seeing this.</p>
</div>

<li class="comment byuser comment-author-dana bypostauthor odd alt depth-2" id="comment-809021">
<article id="article-comment-809021">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c7caa94d71e10eb485999d00c6e9b624?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Dana @ Minimalist Baker" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Dana @ Minimalist Baker</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/grilled-fish-tacos-with-pineapple-cabbage-slaw/?t=1582407402#comment-809021">June 17, 2019 at 12:33 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Vix, thanks for the feedback. We will be continuing to share plant-based recipes, as well as recipes like this one that contain thoughtfully-sourced meat and eggs. We know we won’t please all eaters all the time, but want everyone to feel welcome here (even if every recipe doesn’t suit your needs). </p>
<p>We included a few options to keep this recipe vegan in the notes, and will continue doing so whenever possible moving forward. </p>
<p>If you’d prefer not to see meat or egg recipes, you can adjust your email preferences at the bottom of any email we’ve sent you recently. Or, you can search our vegan-only recipes in our new recipe index <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/recipe-index/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">here</a>.</p>
</div>

					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
			</script>
